    test_withdrawal_requests()¶

    Documentation for tests/prague/eip7002_el_triggerable_withdrawals/test_withdrawal_requests.py::test_withdrawal_requests@6787fbea.

    fill -v tests/prague/eip7002_el_triggerable_withdrawals/test_withdrawal_requests.py::test_withdrawal_requests --fork Prague

    Test making a withdrawal request to the beacon chain.

                    ),

            ],
            id="single_block_single_withdrawal_request_from_eoa_insufficient_fee",

                                valid=False,
                            )
                        ],
                    ),

            ],
            id="single_block_single_withdrawal_request_from_eoa_input_too_short",

def test_withdrawal_requests(
    blockchain_test: BlockchainTestFiller,
    blocks: List[Block],
    pre: Alloc,
):
    """Test making a withdrawal request to the beacon chain."""
    blockchain_test(
        genesis_environment=Environment(),
        pre=pre,
        post={},
        blocks=blocks,
    )
